#Open Artifice Inventions Menu
custom_button = {
	name = artifice_open_inventions
	potential = {
		artifice_invention_has_any_menu_open = no
	}

	trigger = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_country_flag = artificery_unlocked
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = magic_artificery_mixed
				has_country_flag = magic_artificery_artificery_only
			}
			has_artificers_organization_privilege = yes
		}
		is_not_blocked_from_using_invention = yes
	}
	
	effect = {
		set_country_flag = artificery_tab_generic_tier_1_open
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						artifice_has_cultural_invention = yes
						artifice_has_racial_military_invention = yes
						artifice_has_religious_invention = yes
						artifice_has_special_invention = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = has_cultural_special_invention
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_has_unique_invention = yes
				}
				set_country_flag = has_unique_invention
			}
		}
	}

	tooltip = artifice_invention_open_button_tt
}
#Research Button
custom_button = {
	name = artifice_research_inventions
	tooltip = artifice_research_inventions_tt
	potential = { artifice_invention_has_any_menu_open = no }
	trigger = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_country_flag = artificery_unlocked
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = magic_artificery_mixed
				has_country_flag = magic_artificery_artificery_only
			}
			has_artificers_organization_privilege = yes
		}
		is_not_researching_or_blocked_from_researching_invention = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				artifice_invention_researched_all = yes
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = artifice_research.3.x
				always = no
			}
			# this is the tooltip from inside artifice_invention_researched_all
			# (so that we don't re-check the whole giant trigger when we already know we have failed)
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = start_artificery_research_tt
		country_event = {
			id = artifice_research.1
		}
	}
}
#Artificery Fake Capacity Tooltip Button
custom_button = {
	name = artifice_fake_button_capacity_tooltip
	tooltip = artifice_display_capacity_fake_button_tt
	potential = {
		artifice_invention_has_any_menu_open = no
		has_country_flag = artificery_unlocked
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = magic_artificery_mixed
			has_country_flag = magic_artificery_artificery_only
		}
	}
	trigger = {
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = artifice_breakdown_decision_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			update_artifice_points = yes
		}
	}
}

custom_icon = {
	name = artificery_information
	potential = { 
		hidden_trigger = {
			artifice_invention_has_any_menu_open = no 
		}
	}
	#Mage Only
	frame = {
		number = 1
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = magic_artificery_mage_only
		}
	}
	#Mixed Mode
	frame = {
		number = 2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = magic_artificery_mixed
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_korashi_tuners
			}
		}
	}
	#Artificery Only
	frame = {
		number = 3
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = magic_artificery_artificery_only
			NOT = { has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_korashi_tuners }
		}
	}
}

#Unique Tab
custom_button = {
	name = artificery_unique_tab
	tooltip = artificery_unique_selection_tt
	potential = { artifice_invention_has_any_menu_open = yes }
	frame = {
		number = 1 
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = artifice_invention_menu_open_unique_large
					has_country_flag = artifice_invention_menu_open_unique_small
				}
			}
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = artifice_invention_menu_open_unique_large
				has_country_flag = artifice_invention_menu_open_unique_small
			}
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = has_unique_invention_tt
			has_country_flag = has_unique_invention
		}
	}
	effect = { 
		artifice_gui_tab_flag_clearing = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				artifice_invention_is_unique_tab_large_qualifier = yes
			}
			set_country_flag = artifice_invention_menu_open_unique_large
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = artifice_invention_menu_open_unique_small
		}
	}
}
#Insyya Tab
custom_button = {
	name = artificery_insyaa_tab
	tooltip = artificery_insyaa_tab_tt
	potential = { artifice_invention_has_any_menu_open = yes }
	frame = {
		number = 1 
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = artifice_invention_menu_open_insyaa_mechanim
				has_country_flag = artifice_invention_menu_open_insyaa_biological
			}
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 4
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = artifice_invention_menu_open_insyaa_mechanim
				has_country_flag = artifice_invention_menu_open_insyaa_biological
			}
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = stormwall_first_opening
					has_country_modifier = mechanim_administration
					capital_scope = {
						continent = oceania
					}
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = artificery_insyaa_tab_secrets_tt
				always = no
			}
		}
	}
	effect = { 
		artifice_gui_tab_flag_clearing = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = mechanim_administration
			}
			set_country_flag = artifice_invention_menu_open_insyaa_mechanim
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = artifice_invention_menu_open_insyaa_biological
		}
	}
}

#Invention Buttons Tier 1
#Economic Tier 1
custom_button = {
	name = economic_invention_1_1
	tooltip = economic_invention_1_1_tt
	potential = { 
		has_country_flag = artificery_tab_generic_tier_1_open
	}
	frame = {
		number = 3
		trigger = {
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_self_cleaning_parchment
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_self_cleaning_parchment
		}
	}
	frame = { number = 1 }
	trigger = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_self_cleaning_parchment
		}
	}
	effect = { 
		if = {
			limit = {
				artifice_can_select_invention_10 = yes
				NOT = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_self_cleaning_parchment
				}
			}
			set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_self_cleaning_parchment
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				artifice_can_select_invention_10 = no
				NOT = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_self_cleaning_parchment
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
			tooltip = {
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_self_cleaning_parchment
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_self_cleaning_parchment
				unable_to_disable_economic_inventions = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = can_disable_economic_inventions_no_tt
		}
        else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_self_cleaning_parchment
			}
			remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_self_cleaning_parchment
		}
	}
}

#Military Tier 1
custom_button = {
	name = military_invention_1_1
	tooltip = military_invention_1_1_tt
	potential = { 
		has_country_flag = artificery_tab_generic_tier_1_open
	}
	frame = {
		number = 3
		trigger = {
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_portable_turrets
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_portable_turrets
		}
	}
	frame = { number = 1 }
	trigger = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_portable_turrets
		}
	}
	effect = { 
		if = {
			limit = {
				artifice_can_select_invention_10 = yes
				NOT = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_portable_turrets
				}
			}
			set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_portable_turrets
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				artifice_can_select_invention_10 = no
				NOT = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_portable_turrets
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
			tooltip = {
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_portable_turrets
			}
		}
        else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_portable_turrets
			}
			remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_portable_turrets
		}
	}
}

				artifice_can_select_invention_20 = no
				NOT = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arcane_blaster
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
			tooltip = {
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arcane_blaster
			}
		}
        else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arcane_blaster
			}
			remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arcane_blaster
		}
	}
}

#Military Tier 3
custom_button = {
	name = military_invention_3_1
	tooltip = military_invention_3_1_tt
	potential = { 
		has_country_flag = artificery_tab_generic_tier_3_open
	}
	frame = {
		number = 3
		trigger = {
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_black_damestear_bullets
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_black_damestear_bullets
		}
	}
	frame = { number = 1 }
	trigger = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_black_damestear_bullets
		}
	}
	effect = { 
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_30 = yes
					AND = {
						custom_trigger_tooltip = {
							tooltip = artifice_free_upkeep_tt
							has_country_flag = no_upkeep_artifice_invention_black_damestear_bullets
						}
						artifice_has_invention_slot = yes
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_black_damestear_bullets
				}
			}
			set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_black_damestear_bullets
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_30 = yes
					AND = {
						custom_trigger_tooltip = {
							tooltip = artifice_free_upkeep_tt
							has_country_flag = no_upkeep_artifice_invention_black_damestear_bullets
						}
						artifice_has_invention_slot = yes
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_black_damestear_bullets
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
			tooltip = {
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_black_damestear_bullets
			}
		}
        else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_black_damestear_bullets
			}
			remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_black_damestear_bullets
		}
	}
}

#Society Tier 1
custom_button = {
	name = society_invention_1_1
	tooltip = society_invention_1_1_tt
	potential = { 
		has_country_flag = artificery_tab_generic_tier_1_open
	}
	frame = {
		number = 3
		trigger = {
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_viewcatcher
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_viewcatcher
		}
	}
	frame = { number = 1 }
	trigger = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_viewcatcher
		}
	}
	effect = { 
		if = {
			limit = {
				artifice_can_select_invention_10 = yes
				NOT = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_viewcatcher
				}
			}
			set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_viewcatcher
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				artifice_can_select_invention_10 = no
				NOT = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_viewcatcher
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
			tooltip = {
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_viewcatcher
			}
		}
        else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_viewcatcher
				unable_to_disable_society_inventions = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = can_disable_society_inventions_no_tt
		}
        else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_viewcatcher
			}
			remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_viewcatcher
		}
	}
}

#Cultural Inventions
custom_button = {
	name = cultural_invention_1
	tooltip = cultural_invention_1_tt
	potential = {
		has_country_flag = artifice_invention_menu_open_cultural
		artifice_has_cultural_invention = yes
	}
	frame = {
		number = 3
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_artifice_powered_magnate_factories
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_high_velocity_irrigation
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_divendancer_speedboat
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_fine_print_obfuscator
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_superfast_elevators
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_scrapperclaws
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_weather_predicticator
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_prefabricated_city_constructors
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_believable_ruin_bomb
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_wonderous_lunchbox
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_artificial_egg_surrogates
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_kaydhano_powered_vessels
				AND = { #Also an unique invention unlock for Xanzerbexis, extra requirement to prevent UI issues
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_prehensile_tail_attachments
					NOT = { has_country_flag = A49_alternate_prehensile_tail_unlock }
				}
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_wine_ageifier
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_pearl_cultivators
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_war_rigs
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_city_maintenance_bots
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_vernman_hero_tonic
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_automated_translator
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_veykoda_rune_protections
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_warfare_simulator
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_sunspire_pylons
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_mech_building_plates
			}
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					culture_group = alenic
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_artifice_powered_magnate_factories
				}
				AND = {
					is_bulwari_or_zanlibi_culture = yes
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_high_velocity_irrigation
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = businori
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_divendancer_speedboat
					NOT = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = A33 } }
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						primary_culture = crownsman
						primary_culture = ionnic
					}
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_fine_print_obfuscator
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = dwarven
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_superfast_elevators
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = gnollish
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_scrapperclaws
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = eordan_ruinborn_elf
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_weather_predicticator
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = gnomish
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_prefabricated_city_constructors
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = goblin
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_believable_ruin_2_bomb
				}
				AND = {
					culture_is_halfling = yes
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_wondrous_lunchbox
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = harpy
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_artificial_egg_surrogates
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = kheionai_ruinborn_elf
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_kaydhano_powered_vessels
				}
				AND = { #Also an unique invention unlock for Xanzerbexis, extra requirement to prevent UI issues
					culture_group = kobold
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_prehensile_tail_attachments
					NOT = { has_country_flag = A49_alternate_prehensile_tail_unlock }
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = lencori
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_wine_ageifier
				}
				AND = {
					primary_culture = pearlsedger
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_pearl_cultivators
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = taychendi_ruinborn_elf
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_war_rigs
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = triunic
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_city_maintenance_bots
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						culture = vernman
						culture = heartman
					}
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_vernman_hero_tonic
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						primary_culture = west_damerian
						primary_culture = east_damerian
						primary_culture = rogieran
						primary_culture = nurcestiran
						primary_culture = ancardian
						primary_culture = anbenncoster
					}
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_automated_translator
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = ynnic_ruinborn_elf
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_veykoda_rune_protections
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = hobgoblin
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_warfare_simulator
				}
				AND = {
					is_bulwari_elf = yes
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_sunspire_pylons
				}
				AND = {
					has_country_modifier = mechanim_administration
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_mech_building_plates
				}
			}
		}
	}
	frame = { number = 1 }
	trigger = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					culture_group = alenic
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_artifice_powered_magnate_factories
				}
				AND = {
					is_bulwari_or_zanlibi_culture = yes
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_high_velocity_irrigation
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = businori
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_divendancer_speedboat
					NOT = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = A33 } }
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						primary_culture = crownsman

				AND = {
					culture_group = eordan_ruinborn_elf
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_weather_predicticator
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = gnomish
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_prefabricated_city_constructors
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = goblin
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_believable_ruin_2_bomb
				}
				AND = {
					culture_is_halfling = yes
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_wondrous_lunchbox
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = harpy
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_artificial_egg_surrogates
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = kheionai_ruinborn_elf
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_kaydhano_powered_vessels
				}
				AND = { #Also an unique invention unlock for Xanzerbexis, extra requirement to prevent UI issues
					culture_group = kobold
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_prehensile_tail_attachments
					NOT = { has_country_flag = A49_alternate_prehensile_tail_unlock }

				AND = {

					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_war_rigs
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = triunic
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_city_maintenance_bots
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						culture = vernman
						culture = heartman
					}
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_vernman_hero_tonic
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						primary_culture = west_damerian
						primary_culture = east_damerian
						primary_culture = rogieran
						primary_culture = nurcestiran
						primary_culture = ancardian
						primary_culture = anbenncoster
					}
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_automated_translator
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = ynnic_ruinborn_elf
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_veykoda_rune_protections
				}
				AND = {
					culture_group = hobgoblin
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_warfare_simulator
				}
				AND = {
					is_bulwari_elf = yes
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_sunspire_pylons
				}
				AND = {
					has_country_modifier = mechanim_administration
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_mech_building_plates
				}
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				culture_group = alenic
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_30 = yes
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_artifice_powered_magnate_factories
					}
				}
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_artifice_powered_magnate_factories
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_30 = no
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_artifice_powered_magnate_factories
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
				tooltip = {
					set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_artifice_powered_magnate_factories
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_artifice_powered_magnate_factories
					unable_to_disable_economic_inventions = yes
				}
				custom_tooltip = can_disable_economic_inventions_no_tt
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_artifice_powered_magnate_factories
				}
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_artifice_powered_magnate_factories
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_bulwari_or_zanlibi_culture = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_20 = yes
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_high_velocity_irrigation
					}
				}
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_high_velocity_irrigation
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_20 = no
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_high_velocity_irrigation
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
				tooltip = {
					set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_high_velocity_irrigation
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_high_velocity_irrigation
					unable_to_disable_economic_inventions = yes
				}
				custom_tooltip = can_disable_economic_inventions_no_tt
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_high_velocity_irrigation
				}
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_high_velocity_irrigation
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				culture_group = businori
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_30 = yes
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_divendancer_speedboat
					}
				}
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_divendancer_speedboat

					set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_divendancer_speedboat
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {

				}
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_divendancer_speedboat
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = crownsman
					culture = ionnic
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_10 = yes
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_fine_print_obfuscator
					}
				}
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_fine_print_obfuscator
			}
			else_if = {

					artifice_can_select_invention_10 = no
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_fine_print_obfuscator
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention

					set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_fine_print_obfuscator

				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_mech_bureau
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_30 = no
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_mech_bureau
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
				tooltip = {
					set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_mech_bureau
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_mech_bureau
				}
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_mech_bureau
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { culture = sandfang_gnoll }
			if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_20 = yes
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_brine_severer
					}
				}
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_brine_severer
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_20 = no
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_brine_severer
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
				tooltip = {
					set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_brine_severer
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_brine_severer
				}
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_brine_severer
			}
		}
	}
}

#Racial Military Inventions
custom_button = {
	name = racial_military_invention_1
	tooltip = racial_military_invention_1_tt
	potential = {
		has_country_flag = artifice_invention_menu_open_cultural
		artifice_has_racial_military_invention = yes
	}
	frame = {
		number = 3
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_gyrocopters
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_coddorran_powered_exosuit
				AND = { #this one's special b/c kobildzan can unlock it as a Unique invention, so not having this check makes the UI bug out
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_elemental_gunpowder
					has_country_modifier = goblin_military
				}
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_predator_exoskeleton
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_dragonblood_gene_warriors
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_controlled_rage_serum
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_giantshape_warframe
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_mech_lava_cell
			}
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_country_modifier = dwarven_military
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_gyrocopters
				}
				AND = {
					has_country_modifier = gnomish_military
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_coddorran_powered_exosuit
				}
				AND = { #this one's special b/c kobildzan can unlock it as a Unique invention, so not having this check makes the UI bug out
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_elemental_gunpowder
					has_country_modifier = goblin_military
				}
				AND = {
					has_country_modifier = harimari_military
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_predator_exoskeleton
				}
				AND = {
					has_country_modifier = kobold_military
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_dragonblood_gene_warriors
				}
				AND = {
					has_country_modifier = orcish_military
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_controlled_rage_serum
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						has_country_modifier = troll_military
						has_country_modifier = ogre_military
					}
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_giantshape_warframe
				}
				AND = {
					has_country_modifier = mechanim_military
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_mech_lava_cell
				}
			}
		}
	}
	frame = { number = 1 }
	trigger = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_country_modifier = dwarven_military
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_gyrocopters
				}
				AND = {
					has_country_modifier = gnomish_military
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_coddorran_powered_exosuit
				}
				AND = { #this one's special b/c kobildzan can unlock it as a Unique invention, so not having this check makes the UI bug out

					has_country_modifier = goblin_military

				}
				AND = {

				}
				AND = {
					has_country_modifier = orcish_military
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_controlled_rage_serum
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						has_country_modifier = troll_military
						has_country_modifier = ogre_military
					}
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_giantshape_warframe
				}
				AND = {
					has_country_modifier = mechanim_military
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_mech_lava_cell
				}
			}
		}
	}

			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = dwarven_military
			}
			if = {

					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_gyrocopters
					}
				}
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_gyrocopters
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_20 = no
					NOT = {

					}
				}

				}
				AND = {
					has_country_modifier = goblin_military
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_chase_em_rockets
				}
				AND = {
					has_country_modifier = kobold_military
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_dragonscale_plating
				}
				AND = {
					has_country_modifier = mechanim_military
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_mech_fireproof_plating
				}
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = dwarven_military
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_20 = yes
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_platinum_warsuit
					}
				}
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_platinum_warsuit
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_20 = no
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_platinum_warsuit
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
				tooltip = {
					set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_platinum_warsuit
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_platinum_warsuit
				}
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_platinum_warsuit
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = goblin_military
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_30 = yes
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_chase_em_rockets
					}
				}
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_chase_em_rockets
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_30 = no
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_chase_em_rockets
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
				tooltip = {
					set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_chase_em_rockets
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_chase_em_rockets
				}
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_chase_em_rockets
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = kobold_military
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_10 = yes
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_dragonscale_plating
					}
				}
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_dragonscale_plating
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_10 = no
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_dragonscale_plating
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
				tooltip = {
					set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_dragonscale_plating
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_dragonscale_plating
				}
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_dragonscale_plating
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = mechanim_military
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_10 = yes
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_mech_fireproof_plating
					}
				}
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_mech_fireproof_plating
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_10 = no
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_mech_fireproof_plating
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
				tooltip = {
					set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_mech_fireproof_plating
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_mech_fireproof_plating
				}
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_mech_fireproof_plating
			}
		}
	}

#Religion Inventions
custom_button = {
	name = religion_invention_1
	tooltip = religion_invention_1_tt
	potential = {
		has_country_flag = artifice_invention_menu_open_cultural
		artifice_has_religious_invention = yes
	}
	frame = {
		number = 3
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_ancestral_golems
				AND = {
					has_estate_privilege =  artifice_invention_sunbeam_armaments
					NOT = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = F81 } }
				}
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_avatar_supersoldier_serum
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_great_processor
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_fey_spray
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_talking_god_temples
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_wind_invokers
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_artifice_hunting_masks
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_chi_cultivation
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_power_fists
				AND = { #special trigger here b/c kobildzan can unlock lullaby cannons as Unique
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_lullaby_cannon
					religion = skaldhyrric_faith
				}
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_think_quik_drink_mix
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_demonflame_flamethrowers
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_game_of_khet
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_voice_vessels
			}
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 2
		trigger = { #These triggers should be similar to the privileges' `is_valid` trigger
			OR = {
				AND = {
					religion = ancestor_worship
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_ancestral_guardian_golems
				}
				AND = {
					religion_group = bulwari
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_sunbeam_armaments
					NOT = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = F81 } }
				}
				AND = {
					religion_group = cannorian
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_avatar_supersoldier_serum
				}
				AND = {

				}
				AND = {
					religion_group = fey_religion
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_fey_spray
				}
				AND = {

					}
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_talking_god_temples
				}
				AND = {
					religion = irdaeos_worship
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_wind_invokers
				}
				AND = {
					religion = kalun_masks
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_artifice_hunting_masks
				}
				AND = {
					religion = devouring_path
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_chi_cultivation_charm
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						religion = accretive_path
						religion = transmutative_path
					}
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_power_fists
				}
				AND = { # Kobildzan can unlock lullaby cannons as Unique
					religion = skaldhyrric_faith
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_lullaby_cannon
				}
				AND = {
					religion = the_thought

				}
				AND = {
					religion = xhazobkult
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_demonflame_flamethrowers
				}
				AND = {

				}
				AND = {
					religion = the_hunt
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_voice_vessels
				}
			}
		}
	}

custom_button = {
	name = religion_invention_2
	tooltip = religion_invention_2_tt
	potential = {
		has_country_flag = artifice_invention_menu_open_cultural
		OR = {
			religion = ravelian
			religion_group = bulwari
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 3
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_god_fragment_decoder
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_law_books
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_table_war
			}
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					religion = ravelian
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_god_fragment_decoder
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						religion = bulwari_sun_cult
						religion = old_bulwari_sun_cult
					}
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_law_books
				}
				AND = {
					religion = the_jadd
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_table_war
				}
			}
		}
	}
	frame = { number = 1 }
	trigger = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					religion = ravelian
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_god_fragment_decoder
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						religion = bulwari_sun_cult
						religion = old_bulwari_sun_cult
					}
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_law_books
				}
				AND = {
					religion = the_jadd
					has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_table_war
				}
			}
		}
	}
	effect = { 
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = ravelian
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_20 = yes
					NOT = {

			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_20 = no
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_god_fragment_decoder
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
				tooltip = {
					set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_god_fragment_decoder
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_god_fragment_decoder
				}
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_god_fragment_decoder
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					religion = bulwari_sun_cult
					religion = old_bulwari_sun_cult
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_10 = yes
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_law_books
					}
				}
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_law_books
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_10 = no

					}

		has_country_flag = artifice_invention_menu_open_cultural
	}
	frame = {
		number = 3
		trigger = {
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_korashi_drills
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 2
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = korashi_drill_invented_flag
		}
	}
	frame = { number = 1 }
	trigger = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_country_flag = owns_high_temple
		}
	}
	effect = { 
		if = {
			limit = {
				artifice_can_select_invention_10 = yes
				NOT = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_korashi_drills
				}
			}
			set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_korashi_drills
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				artifice_can_select_invention_10 = no
				NOT = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_korashi_drills
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
			tooltip = {
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_korashi_drills
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_korashi_drills
			}
			remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_korashi_drills
		}
	}

				has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_synthetic
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_30 = yes
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_snotfinger_synthetic
					}
				}
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_snotfinger_synthetic
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_30 = no
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_snotfinger_synthetic
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
				tooltip = {
					set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_snotfinger_synthetic
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_snotfinger_synthetic
				}
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_snotfinger_synthetic
			}
		}
	}
}

custom_button = {
	name = insyaa_invention_mechanim_1
	tooltip = artifice_invention_reverse_mechanim
	
	frame = {
		number = 3
		trigger = {
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_reverse_mechanim
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_reverse_mechanim
		}
	}
	frame = { number = 1 }

	trigger = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_reverse_mechanim
		}
		NOT = { has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_industrial_automatories }
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				artifice_can_select_invention_20 = yes
				NOT = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_reverse_mechanim
				}
			}
			set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_reverse_mechanim
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				artifice_can_select_invention_20 = no
				NOT = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_reverse_mechanim
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
			tooltip = {
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_reverse_mechanim
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_reverse_mechanim
			}
			remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_reverse_mechanim
		}
	}
}

custom_button = {
	name = insyaa_invention_mechanim_3
	tooltip = insyaa_invention_mechanim_3_tt
	
	frame = {
		number = 3
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_memory_module
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_behavioral_chip
			}
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 2
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { capital_scope = { continent = oceania } }
				has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_memory_module
			}
			else = {
				has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_behavioral_chip
			}
		}
	}
	frame = { number = 1 }

	trigger = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					capital_scope = {
						continent = oceania
					}
				}
				has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_memory_module
			}
			else = {
				has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_behavioral_chip
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = {
					continent = oceania
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_10 = yes
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_memory_module
					}
				}
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_memory_module
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_10 = no
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_memory_module
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
				tooltip = {
					set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_memory_module
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_memory_module
				}
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_memory_module
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_10 = yes
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_behavioral_chip
					}
				}
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_behavioral_chip
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_10 = no
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_behavioral_chip
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
				tooltip = {
					set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_behavioral_chip
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_behavioral_chip
				}
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_behavioral_chip
			}
		}
	}
}

custom_button = {
	name = insyaa_invention_gene_1
	tooltip = insyaa_invention_gene_1_tt
	
	frame = {
		number = 3
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_crop_enlarge
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_assisted_growth
			}
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 2
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = magic_artificery_artificery_only
				}
				has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_crop_enlarge
			}
			else = {
				has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_assisted_growth
			}
		}
	}
	frame = { number = 1 }
	trigger = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = magic_artificery_artificery_only
				}
				has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_crop_enlarge
			}
			else = {
				has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_assisted_growth
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = magic_artificery_artificery_only
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_10 = yes
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_crop_enlarge
					}
				}
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_crop_enlarge
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_10 = no
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_crop_enlarge
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
				tooltip = {
					set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_crop_enlarge
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_crop_enlarge
				}
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_crop_enlarge
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_10 = yes
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_assisted_growth
					}
				}
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_assisted_growth
			}
			else_if = {

					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
				tooltip = {
					set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_mechanim_deconstructor
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_mechanim_deconstructor
				}
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_mechanim_deconstructor
			}
		}
	}
}

custom_button = {
	name = insyaa_invention_mechanim_tier4_bio
	tooltip = artifice_invention_kraken_galleons
	
	frame = {
		number = 5
		trigger = {
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_kraken_galleons
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 4
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_kraken_galleons
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 3
		trigger = {
			calc_true_if = {
				amount = 2
				has_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_explored_level_3_in_6962
				has_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_explored_level_3_in_3173
				has_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_explored_level_3_in_3551
			}
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_explored_level_3_in_6962
				has_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_explored_level_3_in_3173
				has_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_explored_level_3_in_3551
			}
		}
	}
	frame = { number = 1 }

	trigger = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_explored_level_3_in_6962
				has_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_explored_level_3_in_3173
				has_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_explored_level_3_in_3551
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = you_need_to_find_kraken_galleons
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_kraken_galleons
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_10 = yes
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_kraken_galleons
					}
				}
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_kraken_galleons
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					artifice_can_select_invention_10 = no
					NOT = {
						has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_kraken_galleons
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = artifice_cannot_afford_invention
				tooltip = {
					set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_kraken_galleons
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_kraken_galleons
				}
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_kraken_galleons
		}
		}
		else = {
			tooltip = {
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_kraken_galleons
			}
		}
	}
}

custom_button = {
	name = insyaa_invention_head_1
	tooltip = artifice_invention_head_long_range
	
	frame = {
		number = 3
		trigger = {
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_head_long_range
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_head_long_range
		}
	}
	frame = { number = 1 }

	trigger = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_head_long_range
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = artifice_head_switching_tt
			NOT = { has_country_flag = mechanim_waiting_for_head_event }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_head_long_range
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_head_war_craved
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_head_human_like
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_head_adm_oversight
				set_country_flag = switching_to_artifice_invention_head_long_range

custom_button = {
	name = insyaa_invention_torso_menu
	tooltip = insyaa_invention_torso_menu_tt
	
	frame = {
		number = 3
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = insyaa_invention_torso_menu_open
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = insyaa_invention_torso_menu_unlocked
		}
	}
	frame = { number = 1 }

	trigger = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_country_flag = insyaa_invention_torso_menu_unlocked
		}
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = insyaa_invention_torso_menu_open }
			clr_country_flag = insyaa_invention_torso_menu_open
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = insyaa_invention_torso_menu_open
				clr_country_flag = insyaa_invention_tier4_menu_open
				clr_country_flag = insyaa_invention_head_menu_open
				clr_country_flag = insyaa_invention_chassis_menu_open
				clr_country_flag = insyaa_invention_arms_menu_open
				clr_country_flag = insyaa_invention_legs_menu_open
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_torso_self_repair
				}
				tooltip = {
					remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_torso_self_repair
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_torso_war_craved
				}
				tooltip = {
					remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_torso_war_craved
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_torso_container_part
				}
				tooltip = {
					remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_torso_container_part
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_torso_war_machine
				}
				tooltip = {
					remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_torso_war_machine
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_chassis_soarer_struts

	}

custom_button = {
	name = insyaa_invention_arms_menu
	tooltip = insyaa_invention_arms_menu_tt
	
	frame = {
		number = 3
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = insyaa_invention_arms_menu_open
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = insyaa_invention_arms_menu_unlocked
		}
	}
	frame = { number = 1 }

	trigger = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_country_flag = insyaa_invention_arms_menu_unlocked
		}
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = insyaa_invention_arms_menu_open }
			clr_country_flag = insyaa_invention_arms_menu_open
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = insyaa_invention_arms_menu_open
				clr_country_flag = insyaa_invention_tier4_menu_open
				clr_country_flag = insyaa_invention_head_menu_open
				clr_country_flag = insyaa_invention_torso_menu_open
				clr_country_flag = insyaa_invention_chassis_menu_open
				clr_country_flag = insyaa_invention_legs_menu_open
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arms_dual_pair
				}
				tooltip = {
					remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arms_dual_pair
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arms_stabilizer
				}
				tooltip = {
					remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arms_stabilizer
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arms_construction
				}
				tooltip = {
					remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arms_construction
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arms_sonic_firearm
				}
				tooltip = {
					remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arms_sonic_firearm
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
custom_button = {
	name = insyaa_invention_arms_1
	tooltip = artifice_invention_arms_dual_pair
	
	frame = {
		number = 3
		trigger = {
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arms_dual_pair
		}
	}
	frame = {
		number = 2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_arms_dual_pair
		}
	}
	frame = { number = 1 }

	trigger = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_country_flag = unlocked_artifice_invention_arms_dual_pair
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = artifice_arms_switching_tt
			NOT = { has_country_flag = mechanim_waiting_for_arms_event }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arms_dual_pair
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arms_stabilizer
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arms_construction
				remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arms_sonic_firearm
				set_country_flag = switching_to_artifice_invention_arms_dual_pair
				set_country_flag = mechanim_waiting_for_arms_event
			}
			country_event = {
				id = insyaa_flavour.198
				days = 730
			}
			tooltip = {
				set_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arms_dual_pair
			}
		}
		else = {
			remove_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arms_dual_pair
		}
	}
